=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.

=== Changes in Network Engineering Job Skills and Certifications ===
- Demand for skills in AI-augmented tools like Cisco AI Canvas and Palo Alto Precision AI is growing.
- Certifications such as Cisco DevNet (evolving to CCNA/CCNP Automation) are critical for 2026.
- Zero Trust Architecture (ZTA) expertise, supported by tools like Prisma and Duo, is increasingly required.
